<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обновлять.html>обновля́ть</a> (24362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обновить.html>обнови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обновлять.html>обновля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obnovljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обновить.html>обнови́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to renovate, to refresh, to repair, to make as good as new</li>
<li>to renew, to update</li>
<li>to use/try out for the first time, to give a first trial, <i>(clothes)</i> to wear for the first time, to christen</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обносить.html>обноси́ть</a> (30460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обносить.html>обноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obnosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнести.html>обнести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enclose <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обносить.html>обноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стено́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obnosítʹ</b> stenój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wall</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обносить.html>обноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изгородь.html>и́згородью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obnosítʹ</b> ízgorodʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fence</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обносить.html>обноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перила.html>пери́лами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obnosítʹ</b> perílami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rail in/off</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to serve <i>(round)</i></li>
<li>to miss [pass over] while serving, to fail to serve <i>(to)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обносить.html>обноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obnosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обна́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out (clothing)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break in (clothing) <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to wear to the point of feeling comfortable</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, to feel more comfortable <i>(in an item of clothes, etc)</i></li></ol>

***обнять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обнять.html>обня́ть</a> (2558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнять.html>обня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнимать.html>обнима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hug, to embrace</li>
<li>to engulf, to envelop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is more of a transitive verb in the sense of one person hugging another, and not necessarily a shared or mutual hug implied in the plural conjugations of the English verb (<i>we hugged</i> (each other), <i>you hugged</i> (each other), <i>they hugged</i> (each other), etc.). For implication of mutual hugging, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обниматься.html>обнима́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnimátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обняться.html>обня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obnjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обниматься.html>обнима́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obnimátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объятие.html>объя́тие</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obʺjátije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 14c/c[①].      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:обнимать.html>обнима́ть</a>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-обня-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнять.html>обня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обняться.html>обня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обниматься.html>обнима́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hug, to embrace one another</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнять.html>обня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This verb is reciprocal, meaning a shared hug (<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обняться.html>обнялись</a> = we hugged (each other)) and performing the action in general. For the transitive verb, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнять.html>обня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 14c/c".     <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> прош. вр. муж. <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>возмо́жна</a> устаревающая <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:обняться.html>обнялся́</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:обниматься.html>обнима́ться</a>.

***обо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a> (1616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*o(b)</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃ebʰi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(+ prepositional case)</i>: about, of, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obo</b> mne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">about me</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obo</b> vsex</i> ― <span class="e-translation">about everybody</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(+ accusative case)</i>: against, upon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a></b> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obo</b> štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">upon something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The form <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a></b> is used before <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> (and compound words beginning with чтo); also along with <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> before inflected forms of <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a>. In most cases, use <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> or <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ob</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> instead.
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бо</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a>; неизменяемое <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>Употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> винительным, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> предложным п. <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>Вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́гов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-обо-</b>.
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бо́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, несклоняемое (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 0  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-обо-</b>.

***обобрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обобрать.html>обобра́ть</a> (21373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обобрать.html>обобра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obobrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обирать.html>обира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pick, to collect <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from a tree or garden</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to clean out <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to cheat someone out of their possessions</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gather in folds or ruffles</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rob</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>бра́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>бра́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обобщи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obobščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обобщать.html>обобща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obobščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обобщи́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to generalize, to summarize
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обобщать.html>обобща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опыт.html>о́пыт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obobščátʹ</b> ópyt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to generalize smb's experience</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***обогащать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обогащать.html>обогаща́ть</a> (25301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обогатить.html>обогати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obogatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обогащать.html>обогаща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obogaščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обогатить.html>обогати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enrich, to make rich</li>
<li>to enrich, to make worthy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обогащать.html>обогаща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ниями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obogaščátʹ</b> um znánijami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enrich the mind with knowledge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сство</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обогащать.html>обогаща́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iskússtvo <b>obogaščájet</b> žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">art enriches life</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to concentrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обогащать.html>обогаща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:руда.html>руду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obogaščátʹ</b> rudú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to concentrate/dress the ore</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обогащение.html>обогаще́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obogaščénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:га.html>га</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ща́ть</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обогреть.html>обогре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obogrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обогрева́ть</b>)
